The probability that a user answered "Always" is $30.9 \%$.
The probability that a user did not answer "Never" is $(24.3+13.5+30.9) \% = 68.7 \%$. 
So, the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never" is $\frac{30.9}{68.7}$, which is approximately equal to $0.45$.

### Model: gpt-35-turbo | Prompt: chain_of_thought | Exam: sat-math-100 | Problem 91 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& 2 x-3 y=-14 \\& 3 x-2 y=-6\end{aligned}$$If $(x, y)$ is a solution to the system of equations above, what is the value of $x-y$ ?
Choices:
  A: -20
  B: $\quad-8$
  C: -4
  D: 8
Response 0:
Thought: 
  We want to solve for the value of $x-y$ given the system of linear equations:
  $$\begin{aligned}& 2 x-3 y=-14 \\& 3 x-2 y=-6\end{aligned}$$
  One approach to solve this is to use elimination to eliminate one of the variables in the system of equations. We can then solve for the value of the remaining variable, and use that value to solve for the other variable. Using that value in the expression $x-y$ will give the answer.
  
  To eliminate $y$, we can multiply the first equation by 2, the second equation by 3, and add them:
  $$\begin{aligned}4(2x-3y)&=4(-14)\\
  3(3x-2y)&=3(-6)\end{aligned}$$

  Simplifying the above equations gives:
  $$\begin{aligned}&8x-12y=-56\\&9x-6y=-18\end{aligned}$$

Topic: Math
Question: A line in the $x y$-plane passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Which of the following points lies on the line?
Choices:
  A: $(0,7)$
  B: $(1,7)$
  C: $(7,7)$
  D: $(14,2)$
Response 0:
Thought:
The line passes through origin (0, 0).
The slope of the line is $\frac{1}{7}$ means that it goes up by 1 unit on the y-axis for every 7 units it goes to the right on the x-axis.
We can use the slope-intercept form of a line (y= mx+b) where, m = slope and b = y-intercept.
Since the line goes through the origin, b (y-intercept) is 0 .
Plug in the slope in the equation we get y = $\frac{1}{7} x$.
Now we can check which of these points lie on the line by substituting x and y values in the above equation.
  A: $(0,7)$. It does not lie on the line.
  B: $(1,7)$. It does not lie on the line.
  C: $(7,7)$. It lies on the line.
  D: $(14,2)$. It does not lie on the line.

Therefore,  the point that lies on the line is (7,7).
The answer is C: $(7,7)$

Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We can use the point-slope form of a line to solve this problem: $y = m(x - x_0) + y_0$, 
  where $m$ is the slope of the line, $(x_0, y_0)$ are the coordinates of a known point on the line.
  In this case, $m = \frac{1}{7}$ and the line passes through the origin, $(0,0)$.
  Then, the equation of the line is $y = \frac{1}{7}x$. 
  Let's check which point satisfies the equation of the line.
    For point A: $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 0 = 0 \neq 7$
    For point B: $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 1 = \frac{1}{7} \neq 7$
    For point C: $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 7 = 1 = 7$
    For point D: $y = \frac{1}{7} \cdot 14 = 2 \neq 7$
  Therefore, point C lies on the line.

Thought:

Let C be the amount of Crunchy Grain cereal in the mixture.
Let S be the amount of Super Grain cereal in the mixture.
One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 210 calories for $\frac{3}{4}$ cup. This means one cup of Crunchy Grain cereal provides:

$\frac{210 \ \textrm{calories}}{\frac{3}{4} \ \operatorname{cup}} \times 1 \ \operatorname{cup} = 280 \ \textrm{calories}$

$280 \ \textrm{calories per cup} \times C + 240 \ \textrm{calories per cup} \times S = 270 \ \textrm{calories per cup}$

$28C+24S=27$

$4C+3S=\frac{27}{8}$

$C=1-S$

Substitute C into the previous equation:

$4(1-S)+3S=\frac{27}{8}$

$4-4S+3S=\frac{27}{8}$

$S=\frac{3}{8}$

Therefore, the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{3}{8}$ cup.

Question: $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$The equation above gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet. Which of the following gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$
  D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$
Response 0:
Thought:
The given equation is $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$.
We need to solve the equation for $v$ in terms of $h$, $t$ and $k$.
Taking $16t^{2}$ to the R.H.S, we get:
$$h-k=16t^2-vt$$
Taking out common factor of $t$, we get:
$$h-k=t(16t-v)$$
Solving for $v$, we get:
$$16t-v=\frac{h-k}{t}$$
Therefore, 
$$v=-16t+\frac{h-k}{t}$$
Thus, the answer is A: $v=h+k-16 t$
Action: Answer("A")

$h-k=-16 t^2+vt$
$v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$

  To determine if two lines are perpendicular their slopes must multiply to -1.
  We must put the given equation into slope-intercept form, then the line that we are looking for will need to have a slope that is the negative reciprocal of the first equation.
  The slope-intercept form of a line is $y=mx+b$ where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept.
  The slope $m$ for $-2x+3y=6$ can be found by by solving the equation for $y$ and rearranging it into slope-intercept form. 
  Starting with $-2x+3y=6$:
  $$-2x+3y=6$$
  $$3y=2x+6$$
  $$y=\frac{2}{3}x+2$$
  So, the first line has a slope of $\frac{2}{3}$.
  To find the answer, we need to calculate the slope of each equation and then check the slopes to see which is a negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$.

  $$
  \begin{aligned}
  &\text{A: } 3x+2y=6  \implies y=-\frac{3}{2}x+3 \implies m=-\frac{3}{2} \\
  &\text{B: } 3x+4y=6  \implies y=-\frac{3}{4}x+\frac{3}{2} \implies m=-\frac{3}{4} \\

  \end{aligned}$$

  $$\frac{2}{3} \cdot -\frac{3}{2}=-1 \text{ âŒ}$$

  $$\frac{2}{3} \cdot -\frac{1}{2}=-\frac{1}{3} \text{ âŒ}$$
  $$\frac{2}{3} \cdot -\frac{1}{3}=-\frac{2}{9} $$ Since it does equal -1/ $\frac{2}{9}$ is the negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$, we have a perpendicular line.
  
   So the final answer is D: $2x+6y=3$.

Question: The Downtown Business Association (DBA) in a certain city plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year. There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year. Which function best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now?
Choices:
  A: $y=n x+b$
  B: $y=n x-b$
  C: $y=b(n)^{x}$
  D: $y=n(b)^{x}$
Response 0:

  The DBA is planning to increase its members by $n$ businesses per year.
  There were already $b$ businesses as members of the DBA at the beginning of this year.
  Therefore, the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have after $x$ years can be represented as the sum of the businesses which are currently members and the $n$ businesses that are added each year.
  As $n$ businesses are added for each year, a linear model best describes the relationship between the total number of businesses and the years the DBA plans to have them.
  Therefore, the correct equation is option A, $y=n x+b$.

  The function that meets these requirements is $y=n(b)^{x}$

   $y = nx + b$

  Simplifying this, we get $4x=x(x-3)$
  Therefore, $4x=x^2-3x$ and $x^2-7x=0$
  Thus, $x(x-7)=0 \Rightarrow x=0$ or $x=7$

  Therefore, the only possible value of $x$ is $0$.

Question: $$\begin{aligned}& k x-3 y=4 \\& 4 x-5 y=7\end{aligned}$$In the system of equations above, $k$ is a constant and $x$ and $y$ are variables. For what value of $k$ will the system of equations have no solution?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{12}{5}$
  B: $\frac{16}{7}$
  C: $-\frac{16}{7}$
  D: $-\frac{12}{5}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  There are no solutions to the system of equations when the lines represented by the equations are parallel (the same slope, different $y$-intercepts). If we can transform the equations to the point-slope form, $y - y_1 = m(x - x_1)$, we can find if the slopes are the same, and hence, solve for $k$.

 Calculation:
 Subtract $kx$ from both sides of the first equation to get: $$-3y = -kx + 4 $$ Divide by -3: $$y = \frac{k}{3}x - \frac{4}{3}$$ Subtract 4x from both sides of the second equation to get: $$-5y = -4x + 7 $$ Divide by -5: $$y = \frac{4}{5}x - \frac{7}{5}$$
 
 By comparing the equations in slope-intercept form, the slopes are equal if:$$ \frac{k}{3} = \frac{4}{5} \Rightarrow k = \frac{12}{5}.$$
 If $k = \frac{12}{5}$, the two equations become identical. Therefore, there will be no solution for the system. 

Answer: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  For a system of linear equations to have no solution, the lines must be parallel.
  We can check if two lines are parallel by comparing their slopes.
  To compare the slopes, we can rearrange each equation to the form $y = mx + b$.
  For the first equation, we have $-3y = -kx + 4 \Rightarrow y = \frac{k}{3}x - \frac{4}{3}$.
  For the second equation, we have $-5y = -4x + 7 \Rightarrow y = \frac{4}{5}x - \frac{7}{5}$.
  The slope of the first line is $\frac{k}{3}$ and the slope of the second line is $\frac{4}{5}$.
  For the two lines to be parallel, their slopes must be equal.
  Therefore, we need to solve $\frac{k}{3} = \frac{4}{5}$.
  Solving for $k$, we get $k = \frac{12}{5}$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $\frac{12}{5}$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
We can solve this system of equations using algebra. If we try to solve this system of equation using elimination method, we first have to multiply the first equation by $4$ so that we can eliminate $x$. However, we can see that the equation of $y$ is not the same. Therefore, we can solve for $k$ by making a determinant equal to zero.

$$\begin{vmatrix} k & -3 \\ 4 & -5 \\ \end{vmatrix} = k \times (-5) - (-3) \times 4 = -5k + 12 $$

If we want to find the value of $k$ which has no solution, then we need to make sure that this system of equations has no solutions, which means that the determinant should be equal to zero.

$$-5k+12=0$$
$$k=\frac{12}{5}$$

If $k$ is equal to $12/5$, this system of equation will have no solution.
